<div>

<p><span style='color:red'>Latest update Feb 28, 2013: use topology_dimension
attribute rather than dimension, as suggested by Jonathan Gregory <a
href="http://www.met.rdg.ac.uk/~jonathan/CF_metadata/ugrid_gridspec.html">here</a>.</span><br>
Update Sep 12, 2012: closed clockwise discussion, explained meaning of
Optionally required attributes.<br>
You can use the following shorthand <tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'><a
href="http://bit.ly/ugrid_cf">http://bit.ly/ugrid_cf</a></span></tt> to refer
to this page.</p>

<p>PLEASE NOTE: The title of this page suggests that this is only a proposal by
Deltares. However, the support for this proposal is already much wider than
that (see the <a href="http://groups.google.com/group/ugrid-interoperability">UGRID
Google Group</a>) and is under active discussion with an important subset of
the CF community. We keep the current title only such that it does not break
any existing external links to this information.</p>

<p>The section of creating mosaics of meshes has been moved to this <a
href="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/display/NETCDF/Mosaics+of+meshes"
title="Mosaics of meshes">child page</a>. Since experience with unstructured grid
mosaics is still limited, and demand is low, the mosaics are not yet part of
the current proposal.</p>

<h2><a name=DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat><span style='font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Introduction.<o:p></o:p></span></a></h2>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>This
page describes a proposal for storing unstructured (or flexible mesh) model
data in a netCDF file. Our focus is on data for environmental applications and
hence we start from the </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>CF-conventions</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> which has been
the standard in climate research for many years, and is increasingly adopted by
others as the metadata standard for netCDF, see e.g. </span><a
href="http://www.esdswg.org/spg/rfc/esds-rfc-021"><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>NASA Standards Process Group</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> and </span><a
href="http://www.opengeospatial.org/standards/netcdf"><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>OGC</span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>. The CF conventions allow you to
define values at points, and the associated coordinates may have </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt> attributes to indicate a spatial
extent bigger than a single point. A two-dimensional array of points, encodes a
structured topology but the CF conventions do not yet provide the means to
define an unstructured topology. That's what this proposal adds.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>In its
most basic form unstructured data may be stored as data defined at a series of
points, the CF-conventions are then sufficient. However, it is often useful or
even necessary to also know the topology of the underlying unstructured mesh:
is it a 1D network, a 2D triangular mesh or more flexible mixed
triangle/quadrilateral mesh, a 2D mesh with vertical layers, or a fully
unstructured 3D mesh. This document describes the attribute conventions for
storing the mesh topology and for associating variables with (specific
locations on) the mesh topology. The conventions have been designed to store
the output data of a combined 1D-2D-3D flow model with staggered data, but the
metadata for a simple 1D network or 2D triangular mesh doesn't suffer from the
genericity needed for the most complex models.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Due to
the wide variety in unstructured mesh models, some relevant concepts have not
yet been worked out in detail. This includes the following concepts:</span></p>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>adaptive mesh topology (this
     could be supported by defining a </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>time_concatenation</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute for a time-series of mesh topologies)<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>higher order element data; for
     an idea how such data could be stored see this other </span></span><a
     href="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/display/NETCDF/Finite+Element+based+CF+proposal+for+Unstructured+Grid+data+model"
     title="Finite Element based CF proposal for Unstructured Grid data model"><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>proposal</span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>subgrid data; the netCDF pages
     by the BAW contain some proposals on this topic (</span></span><a
     href="http://www.baw.de/methoden/index.php5/NetCDF"><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>see
     their pages (in German)</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>).<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>3D fully unstructured meshes
     (included but still limited in scope).<br>
     See also a related </span></span><a
     href="https://svn.pnl.gov/gcrm/wiki/DataModelProposal"><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>proposal</span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     for an unstructured mesh data model by Jeff Daily at PNNL.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>More
details can be found in the various sections below:</span></p>

<div>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;

     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span><a

<h2><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Topology.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h2>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Naming
conventions for geometrical elements.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Inspired
by Wikipedia's definition of </span><a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_topology"><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>network topology</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>, we define the
mesh topology here as the interconnection of various geometrical elements of the
mesh. The pure interconnectivity is independent of georeferencing the
individual geometrical elements, but for the practical applications for which
we are defining this CF extension, we'll always add coordinate data. Within a
mesh, one can distinguish 0-, 1-, 2- and 3-dimensional elements. We need some
names to identify these four types of elements; after discussion we propose the
following names:</span></p>

<div>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=0 cellspacing=3 cellpadding=0
 style='mso-cellspacing:1.5pt;mso-yfti-tbllook:1184'>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes'>

  style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Dimensionality
  <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>
  </td>
  <span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span>
  <td style='padding:.75pt .75pt .75pt .75pt'>

  style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Proposed

  style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>node

  point, a coordinate pair or triplet: the most basic element of the topology.<br>
  The word node seems to be more commonly used than the alternative
  &quot;vertex&quot;. <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  </td>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span

  </td>

  <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

  </td>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='color:red;mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=16 height=16
id="_x0000_i1039"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"></span><span
style='color:red'>In favor of simpler code for interpreting compliant files, we
have dropped to use of the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:red'>locations</span></tt><span style='color:
red'> attribute which allowed the user to specify his/her own names for nodes,
edges, faces and volumes.</span></span></p>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>1D
network topology.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
topology information is stored as attributes to a dummy variable (in the
example below called &quot;Mesh1&quot;) with </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>cf_role</span></tt>
mesh_topology.</span></p>

<div>

  <td style='padding:.75pt .75pt .75pt .75pt'>

  style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>edge_coordinates
  <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  </td>
  <span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span>
  <td style='padding:.75pt .75pt .75pt .75pt'><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></td>
  <span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span>
 </tr>

</div>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>topology_dimension</span></tt> indicates the highest
dimensionality of the geometric elements; for a 1D network this should be 1.
The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> points to the auxiliary
coordinate variables representing the node locations (latitude, longitude, and
optional elevation or other coordinates). These auxiliary coordinate variables
will have length nNodes. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> points to an index
variable identifying for every edge to the indices of its begin and end nodes.
The connectivity array will thus be a matrix of size nEdges x 2. For the
indexing one may use either 0- or 1-based indexing; the convention used should
be specified using a </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh1_edge_nodes in the example below). Consistent with the
CF-conventions </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>compression</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> option, the
connectivity indices are 0-based by default.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='color:red;mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=16 height=16
id="_x0000_i1038"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"></span><span
style='color:red'>The option to support both 0- and 1-based indexing was
introduced to be able to support existing files with 1-based index tables using
ncML.</span> See </span><a href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this section on
0-/1-based indexing</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> for more
details.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
mesh_topology may optionally include an </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_coordinates</span></tt> attribute which points to
the auxiliary coordinate variables associated with the characteristic location
of the edge (commonly the midpoint). These auxiliary coordinate variables will
have length nEdges, and may have in turn a </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt>
attribute that specifies the bounding coordinates of the edge (thereby
duplicating the data in the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> variables).</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='color:red;mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=16 height=16
id="_x0000_i1037"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"></span><span
style='color:red'>This use of the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:red'>bounds</span></tt><span style='color:red'>
attribute is consistent with the CF-convention on the use of </span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:red'>bounds</span></tt><span style='color:red'>
for multi-dimensional coordinate variables with p-sided cells, but it may not
strictly be supported by the CF-convention right now.</span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1036"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/network.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276458471000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/network.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276458471000"></span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Example:</span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>dimensions:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh1_node = 5 ; // nNodes<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh1_edge = 4 ; // nEdges<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Two = 2;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>variables:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>// Mesh topology<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>integer Mesh1 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:cf_role = &quot;mesh_topology&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:long_name = &quot;Topology data of 1D network&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:topology_dimension = 1 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>           </span>Mesh1:node_coordinates = &quot;Mesh1_node_x Mesh1_node_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

</div>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>*The
&quot;Optionally required&quot; attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt>
is required only if you want to store data on the edges (i.e. if you mind the
numbering order of the edges).</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>topology_dimension</span></tt> indicates the highest
dimensionality of the geometric elements; for a 2-dimensional (triangular) mesh
this should be 2. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> points to the auxiliary
coordinate variables representing the node locations (latitude, longitude, and
optional elevation or other coordinates). These auxiliary coordinate variables
will have length nNodes. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> points to an index
variable identifying for every face (here consistently triangle) the indices of
its three corner nodes. The corner nodes should be specified in anticlockwise
(also referred to as counterclockwise) direction as viewed from above
(consistent with the CF-convention for </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt> of p-sided cells. The connectivity
array will thus be a matrix of size nFaces x 3. For the indexing one may use
either 0- or 1-based indexing; the convention used should be specified using a </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_nodes in the example below). Consistent with the
CF-conventions </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>compression</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> option, the
connectivity indices are 0-based by default. See </span><a
href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this
section on 0-/1-based indexing</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> for more
details.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>In case
you want to define variables on the edges of the triangular mesh topology you
need to specify the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> attribute to map
edges to nodes. Although the face to node mapping implicitly also defines the
location of the edges, it does not specify the global numbering of the edges.
Again the indexing convention of </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> should be specified
using the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh2_edge_nodes in the example below) and 0-based indexing is
the default.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Optionally
the topology may have the following attributes:</span></p>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l4 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every face (here
     consistently triangle) the indices of its three edges. The edges should be
     specified in anticlockwise direction as viewed from above. This
     connectivity array will thus be a matrix of size nFaces x 3. Again the
     indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_edges in the example
     below) and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l4 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_face_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying pairs of faces (here
     consistently triangle) that share an edge, i.e. are neighbors. <span
     style='color:red'>TODO: CHECK DEFINITION</span> This connectivity array
     will thus be a matrix of size nFacePairs x 2. Again the indexing
     convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_face_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_links in the example
     below) and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l4 level1 lfo3;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     and/or </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to the auxiliary coordinate variables associated with the
     characteristic location of the faces and edges. These auxiliary coordinate
     variables will have length nFaces and nEdges respectively, and may have in
     turn a </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> attribute that specifies the
     bounding coordinates of the face or edge (thereby duplicating the data in
     the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     variables).<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ul>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>2D
flexible mesh (mixed triangles, quadrilaterals, etc.) topology.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The case
of a 2D mesh with mixed face sizes is identical to the 2D triangular mesh
discussed above with the exception that not all faces have the same number of
nodes. To support this variability we may use in the future a ragged array, but
here we propose to use _FillValue to indicate faces with smaller number of
nodes than the arrays allow.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
topology information is stored as attributes to a dummy variable (in the
example below called &quot;Mesh2&quot;) with </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>cf_role</span></tt>
mesh_topology.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>*The
&quot;Optionally required&quot; attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt>
is required only if you want to store data on the edges (i.e. if you mind the
numbering order of the edges).</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>topology_dimension</span></tt> indicates the highest
dimensionality of the geometric elements; for a 2-dimensional mesh this should
be 2. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> points to the auxiliary
coordinate variables representing the node locations (latitude, longitude, and
optional elevation or other coordinates). These auxiliary coordinate variables
will have length nNodes. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> points to an index
variable identifying for every face the indices of its corner nodes. The corner
nodes should be specified in anticlockwise direction as viewed from above
(consistent with the CF-convention for </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt> of p-sided cells. The connectivity
array will be a matrix of size nFaces x MaxNumNodesPerFace; if a face has less
corner nodes than MaxNumNodesPerFace then the last node indices shall be equal
to </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt> (which should obviously be
larger than the number of nodes in the mesh). For the indexing one may use
either 0- or 1-based indexing; the convention used should be specified using a </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_nodes in the example below). Consistent with the
CF-conventions </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>compression</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> option, the
connectivity indices are 0-based by default. See </span><a
href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this
section on 0-/1-based indexing</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> for more
details.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>In case
you want to define variables on the edges of the 2D mesh topology you need to
specify the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> attribute to map
edges to nodes. Although the face to node mapping implicitly also defines the
location of the edges, it does not specify the global numbering of the edges.
Again the indexing convention of </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> should be specified
using the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh2_edge_nodes in the example below) and 0-based indexing is
the default.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Optionally
the topology may have the following attributes:</span></p>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every face the indices of
     its edges. The edges should be specified in anticlockwise direction as
     viewed from above. This connectivity array will be a matrix of size nFaces
     x MaxNumNodesPerFace. Again, if a face has less corners/edges than
     MaxNumNodesPerFace then the last edge indices shall be equal to </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     and the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_edges in the example
     below) and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_face_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying pairs of faces that share an
     edge, i.e. are neighbors. <span style='color:red'>TODO: CHECK DEFINITION</span>
     This connectivity array will thus be a matrix of size nFacePairs x 2.
     Again the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_face_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable (i.e. Mesh2_face_links in the example
     below) and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     and/or </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to the auxiliary coordinate variables associated with the
     characteristic location of the faces and edges. These auxiliary coordinate
     variables will have length nFaces and nEdges respectively, and may have in
     turn a </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
     mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> attribute that specifies the
     bounding coordinates of the face or edge (thereby duplicating the data in
     the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     variables).<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='color:red;mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=16 height=16
id="_x0000_i1034"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"></span><span
style='color:red'>The use of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:red'>_FillValue</span></tt><span
style='color:red'> to indicate faces with less nodes than MaxNumNodesPerFace
extends to the coordinate bounds variables; this is an extension of the current
convention.</span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1033"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/mixedmesh.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/mixedmesh.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"></span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Example:</span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>dimensions:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        span>nMesh2_node = 5 ; // nNodes<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_edge = 6 ; // nEdges<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_face = 2 ; // nFaces<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_face_links = 1 ; // nFacePairs<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh2_face_nodes = 4 ; // MaxNumNodesPerFace<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Two = 2 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>variables:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>// Mesh topology<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>integer Mesh2 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2:cf_role = &quot;mesh_topology&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2:long_name = &quot;Topology data of 2D unstructured mesh&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>         </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>       </span>Mesh2:topology_dimension = 2 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>3D
layered mesh topology.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>For a 3D
layered unstructured mesh topology this proposal follows the approach of the
existing CF-conventions for structured meshes: horizontal and vertical
dimensions are treated separately. For the horizontal plane a 2D unstructured
mesh topology is defined, which is extruded in the vertical direction by means
of a </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#vertical-coordinate"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>vertical
coordinate</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>. The example
below matches the example in the previous section combined with a vertical
coordinate according CF-conventions. This example introduces also the
attributes </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>mesh</span></tt> and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>location</span></tt>
on the 2D variables &quot;Mesh2_surface&quot; and &quot;Mesh2_depth&quot;. For
more information about these attributes see the </span><a
href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>data
definition</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> section below.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1032"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/layered.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/layered.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"></span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Example:</span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>dimensions:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_node = 6 ; // nNodes<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_edge = 7 ; // nEdges<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_face = 2 ; // nFaces<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh2_face_links = 1 ; // nFacePairs<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh2_face_nodes = 4 ; // MaxNumNodesPerFace<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Mesh2_layers = 10 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Two = 2 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>variables:<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>// Mesh topology<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_surface:location = &quot;face&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_surface:coordinates = &quot;Mesh2_face_x Mesh2_face_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre></div>

</div>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>fully
3D unstructured (i.e. non-layered) mesh topology.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>For a
fully 3D unstructured mesh topology we extend the hierarchy of nodes, edges and
faces to volumes. Contrary to layered case this type of mesh requires a fully
3D specification of the mesh; hence we not only need latitude and longitude
coordinates but also some kind of elevation coordinate (<span style='color:
red'>this probably requires a new standard name</span>).</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
topology information is stored as attributes to a dummy variable (in the
example below called &quot;Mesh3D&quot;) with </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>cf_role</span></tt>
mesh_topology.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>*The
&quot;Optionally required&quot; attributes </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt>
and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> are required only
if you want to store data on the edges or faces respectively (i.e. if you mind
the numbering order of the edges/faces).</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>topology_dimension</span></tt> indicates the highest
dimensionality of the geometric elements; for a fully 3-dimensional
unstructured mesh this should be 3. The attribute </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> points to the auxiliary
coordinate variables representing the node locations (latitude, longitude,
elevation and optional other coordinates). These auxiliary coordinate variables
will have length nNodes. The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_node_connectivity</span></tt> points to an
index variable identifying for every volume the indices of its corner nodes. For
faces in the horizontal plane, it was possible to prescribe the order of the
nodes, but this is not possible for the nodes of generic 3D volumes. For this
reason we introduce an additional attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_shape_type</span></tt>
which points to a flag variable that specifies for every volume its shape:</span></p>

<div>

</div>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>These
four volume shapes are the ones most commonly used. More shapes can be added;
and if necessary, it's possible to add a generic shape type which allows for
specification of the volume shape indirectly via </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_face_connectivity</span></tt>
and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> variables. Such a
generic shape is not included in this proposal since there is no practical need
for such feature at this time.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='color:red;mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=16 height=16
id="_x0000_i1031"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/images/icons/emoticons/warning.gif"></span><span
style='color:red'>If all volumes have the same shape type, then the shape typed
could be determined based on the number of nodes per volume. Another option
could be to allow the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;color:red'>volume_shape_type</span></tt><span
style='color:red'> to specify the shape type directly rather than pointing to a
variable. However, for the time being we assume that the currently proposed
volume shape type variable doesn't have too much impact on the performance.</span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
order in which the corner nodes of a volume are specified is fixed given its
shape; this approach is common in 3D modeling, see e.g. </span><a
href="http://www.openfoam.com/docs/user/mesh-description.php#x23-1350072"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this graph in the
OpenFOAM documentation</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> and </span><a
href="http://www.vtk.org/Wiki/index.php?title=ParaView/Users_Guide/VTK_Data_Model"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>PARAVIEW</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> or </span><a
href="http://www.vtk.org/doc/release/5.8/html/a00294.html"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>VTK</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> documentation.
The </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_node_connectivity</span></tt> array will be a
matrix of size nVolumes x MaxNumNodesPerVolume; if a volume has less corner
nodes than MaxNumNodesPerVolume then the last node indices shall be equal to </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt> (which should obviously be
larger than the number of nodes in the mesh). For the indexing one may use
either 0- or 1-based indexing; the convention used should be specified using a </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable (i.e. Mesh3D_vol_nodes in the example below). Consistent with the
CF-conventions </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>compression</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> option, the
connectivity indices are 0-based by default. See </span><a
href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this
section on 0-/1-based indexing</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> for more
details.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>In case
you want to define variables on the faces or edges of the 3D mesh topology you
need to specify the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> or </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> attribute,
respectively, to map faces or edges to nodes. Although the volume to node
mapping implicitly also defines the location of the faces and edges, it does
not specify their global numbering. Again the indexing convention of </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt> and </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_node_connectivity</span></tt> should be specified
using the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable and 0-based indexing is the default.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Optionally
the topology may have the following attributes:</span></p>

<ul type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_face_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every volume the indices of
     its faces. The order in which the face indices should be specified is
     determined by the volume geometry type. This connectivity array will be a
     matrix of size nVolumes x MaxNumFacesPerVolume. If a volume has less faces
     than MaxNumFacesPerVolume then the last face indices shall be equal to </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     and the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every volume the indices of
     its edges. The order in which the edge indices should be specified is
     determined by the volume geometry type. This connectivity array will be a
     matrix of size nVolumes x MaxNumEdgesPerVolume. Again, if a volume has
     less edges than MaxNumEdgesPerVolume then the last edge indices shall be
     equal to </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     and the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_volume_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying pairs of volumes that share a
     face, i.e. are neighbors. This connectivity array will thus be a matrix of
     size nVolumePairs x 2. As usual the indexing convention of </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_volume_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable (i.e. Mesh3D_vol_links in the example
     below) and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every face the indices of
     its edges. The edges should be specified in anticlockwise direction as
     viewed from above. This connectivity array will be a matrix of size nFaces
     x MaxNumNodesPerFace. As always, if a face has less corners/edges than
     MaxNumNodesPerFace then the last edge indices shall be equal to </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     and the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_edge_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to an index variable identifying for every face the indices of
     its nodes. The nodes should be specified in either clockwise or
     anticlockwise order. This connectivity array will be a matrix of size
     nFaces x MaxNumNodesPerFace. Again, if a face has less corners/edges than
     MaxNumNodesPerFace then the last node indices shall be equal to </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>_FillValue</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     and the indexing convention of </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_node_connectivity</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     should be specified using the </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute to the index variable and 0-based indexing is the default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;
     mso-list:l2 level1 lfo5;tab-stops:list .5in'><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>volume_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,
     </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     and/or </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>edge_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     pointing to the auxiliary coordinate variables associated with the
     characteristic location of the volumes, faces and edges. These auxiliary
     coordinate variables will have length nVolumes, nFaces and nEdges
     respectively, and may have in turn a </span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
     DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     attribute that specifies the corner coordinates of the volume, face or
     edge (thereby duplicating the data in the </span></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
     style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt></span><span
     style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
     style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
     variables). The order in which the corner coordinates of the volumes is
     given by the volume geometry type.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ul>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh3D_face = 16 ; // nFaces<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh3D_vol<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>= 4 ; // nVolumes<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh3D_vol_links = 4 ; // nVolumePairs<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh3D_face_nodes = 4 ; // MaxNumNodesPerFace<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh3D_vol_nodes<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>= 8 ; // MaxNumNodesPerVolume<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh3D_vol_edges<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>= 12 ; // MaxNumEdgesPerVolume<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMaxMesh3D_vol_faces<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>= 6 ; // MaxNumFacesPerVolume<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Two = 2 ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:face_node_connectivity = &quot;Mesh3D_face_nodes&quot; ; // attribute required if variables will be defined on faces<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:edge_node_connectivity = &quot;Mesh3D_edge_nodes&quot; ; // attribute required if variables will be defined on edges<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:edge_coordinates = &quot;Mesh3D_edge_x Mesh3D_edge_y Mesh3D_edge_z&quot; ; // optional attribute (requires edge_node_connectivity)<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:face_coordinates = &quot;Mesh3D_face_x Mesh3D_face_y Mesh3D_face_z&quot; ; // optional attribute (requires face_node_connectivity)<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:volume_coordinates = &quot;Mesh3D_vol_x Mesh3D_vol_y Mesh3D_vol_z&quot; ; // optional attribute<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:volume_face_connectivity = &quot;Mesh3D_vol_faces&quot; ; // optional attribute (requires face_node_connectivity)<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:volume_edge_connectivity = &quot;Mesh3D_vol_edges&quot; ; // optional attribute (requires edge_node_connectivity)<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh3D:face_edge_connectivity = &quot;Mesh3D_face_edges&quot; ; // optional attribute (requires face_node_connectivity and edge_node_connectivity)<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
