<h2><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Data
defined on unstructured meshes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h2>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>According
to CF-conventions a variable defined on a <em><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>structured</span></em>
mesh is specified as</span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>double waterlevel(time,nmax,mmax) ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>waterlevel:standard_name = &quot;sea_surface_height_above_geoid&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>waterlevel:units = &quot;m&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>waterlevel:coordinates = &quot;lat lon&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre></div>

</div>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attribute refers to the
variables that contain the latitude and longitude coordinates. For a
curvilinear grid these variables will share two spatial dimensions, here </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>nmax</span></tt> and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>mmax</span></tt>:
lat(nmax,mmax) and lon(nmax,mmax). In numerical models the various quantities
are often computed at different locations of the mesh: staggered data. The
standard CF-conventions don't offer specific support for this functionality and
thus for every stagger location coordinates need to be provided separately:
cell center coordinates, corner point coordinates, u-flux point coordinates,
and v-flux point coordinates. The underlying topology of the mesh, i.e. how
these coordinates (variable definition locations) relate to each other isn't
stored in the file. This shortcoming is to some degree solved by the </span><a
href="http://www.gfdl.noaa.gov/~vb/gridstd/gridstd.html"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>gridspec</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> proposal by
Balaji. We introduce here attributes that link to the topological data defined
above.</span></p>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Data
variables.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The use
of the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attribute is copied from the
CF-conventions. It is used to map the values of variables defined on the
unstructured meshes directly to their location: latitude, longitude and
optional elevation. To map the variable onto the topology of the underlying
mesh, two new attributes have been introduced. First, the attribute </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>mesh</span></tt> points to the mesh_topology variable
containing the meta-data attributes of the mesh on which the variable has been
defined. Second, the attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>location</span></tt> points to the (stagger) location
within the mesh at which the variable is defined. Note that in this example the
</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attribute is redundant since
the coordinates could also be obtained by using the </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>face_coordinates</span></tt> attribute of the
&quot;Mesh2&quot; variable.</span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>double Mesh2_waterlevel(time,nMesh2_face) ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_waterlevel:standard_name = &quot;sea_surface_height_above_geoid&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_waterlevel:units = &quot;m&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_waterlevel:mesh = &quot;Mesh2&quot;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_waterlevel:location = &quot;face&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_waterlevel:coordinates = &quot;Mesh2_face_x Mesh2_face_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre></div>

</div>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Volume
and flux variables.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The same
mesh geometry can be used in different ways to schematize the hydrodynamic
volumes and fluxes. Let's take a simple triangular mesh. From a finite volume
point of view this mesh will generally be interpreted as consisting of two
volumes with triangular base. However, others may use a continuous Galerkin
finite element method that can be shown to be equivalent to a subdivision into
four volumes. In the former case the two faces correspond to volumes and the
fluxes <em><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>cross</span></em> the
edges. In the latter case the volumes are defined surrounding the four nodes
and the fluxes are directed <em><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>along</span></em>
the edges. The two abbreviated ncdumps below show how the basic 2D triangular
mesh definition can be extended to include this data. The coordinate variables
for the volume data now include </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>bounds</span></tt> attributes to define the surface
area of the volumes. Note the subtle difference in the long names between the
flux variables in the two cases; the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>standard_name</span></tt> attribute has to make a more
formal distinction between the two cases.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1029"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/fv_triangles.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/fv_triangles.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"></span><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1028"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/fv_nodes.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/fv_nodes.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460147000"></span></span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Variant
1: Volume at faces:</span></p>

style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_volumes:units = &quot;m3&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_volumes:mesh = &quot;Mesh2&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_volumes:location = &quot;node&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_volumes:coordinates = &quot;Mesh2_node_x Mesh2_node_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>double Mesh2_fluxes(nMesh2_edge) ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_fluxes:long_name = &quot;flux along edge&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_fluxes:units = &quot;m3 s-1&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_fluxes:mesh = &quot;Mesh2&quot;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_fluxes:location = &quot;edge&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre><pre><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh2_fluxes:coordinates = &quot;Mesh2_edge_x Mesh2_edge_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></span></pre></div>

</div>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Location
index set.<o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Some
variables may only be defined at specific locations within the mesh, e.g. only
at boundary points or at special locations like weirs and gates. To save space
and to improve readability, the concept of a location_index_set is introduced.
It is basically identical to the </span><a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering"><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>compression</span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> option in the
the CF-conventions except for the fact that the compression works on a (set of)
orthogonal coordinate dimension(s) and the location_index_set works on a
topology location.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>The
location index set is an integer variable that contains the indices of the
locations at which a specific quantity is defined. The example below defines a
location index set &quot;Mesh1_set&quot; as a subset of the &quot;node&quot;s
of Mesh1 (red points). The attribute </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>location_index_set</span></tt> of the variable
&quot;Mesh_waterlevel&quot; points to this index set and the </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attribute points to the
corresponding (subset) of latitude and longitude coordinates. The </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>mesh</span></tt> and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>location</span></tt>
attributes of the location_index_set variable are required; the </span><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attribute is optional. Note
that the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>coordinates</span></tt> attributes on both
&quot;Mesh1_cell&quot; and &quot;Mesh1_waterlevel&quot; are again redundant
since the coordinates could also be obtained by using the index set
&quot;Mesh1_set&quot; and the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>node_coordinates</span></tt> attribute of the
&quot;Mesh1&quot; variable. Consistent with all other index variables defined
here, the indexing convention of the location index set should be specified
using the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute to the index
variable and 0-based indexing is the default. See </span><a
href="#DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGridda"><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>this
section on 0-/1-based indexing</span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'> for more
details.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'>Contrary
to a coordinate variable, the index set doesn't have to be monotonic. So, it
can be used for creating subsets of the original locations as well as for
renumbering the locations. If the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>location_index_set</span></tt> attribute is used on a
variable, then the </span><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>mesh</span></tt> and </span><span style='mso-bookmark:
DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>location</span></tt>
attributes should not also be used on that variable.</span></p>

<p><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32 id="_x0000_i1027"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/network_location_map.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460146000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/network_location_map.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1276460146000"></span></span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'><span

<span style='mso-bookmark:DeltaresCFproposalforUnstructuredGriddat'></span>

<h2><span style='font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>0-/1-based
indexing<o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p>The indexing using by the CF <a
href="http://cf-pcmdi.llnl.gov/documents/cf-conventions/1.4/cf-conventions.html#compression-by-gathering">compression</a>
option is 0-based. Therefore, it is most consistent for this CF extension for
unstructured data to also use 0-based indexing, which means that points, edges,
faces and volumes will be numbered starting with 0. This convention is
consistent with languages like C and Java, but unlike FORTRAN and MATLAB. Since
many of the unstructured models have been programed in FORTRAN and legacy
netCDF files exist that use 1-based indexing (which could be upgraded to be
consistent with this new proposal using ncML if 1-based indexing were allowed),
we propose to support both 0- and 1-based indexing by means of the <tt><span
style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt> attribute. You will find below
two examples of the same network geometry using either 0- or 1-based indexing.
Switching between 0- and 1-based indexing is as easy as adding 1 to or
subtracting 1 from the indices upon reading or writing depending on the setting
of <tt><span style='font-size:10.0pt'>start_index</span></tt>; allowing both
options should only have a minor impact on the reading routines and no effect
at all on the rest of your code.</p>

<p>Example of 0-based indexing:</p>

<p><span style='mso-no-proof:yes'><img border=0 width=32 height=32
id="_x0000_i1026"
src="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/0-based_index.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1340607595000"
alt="https://publicwiki.deltares.nl/download/attachments/41156627/0-based_index.png?version=1&amp;modificationDate=1340607595000"></span></p>

<div>

<div><pre><span style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>dimensions:<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh1_node = 5 ; // nNodes<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>nMesh1_edge = 4 ; // nEdges<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>Two = 2;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>variables:<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>// Mesh topology<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>integer Mesh1 ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:cf_role = &quot;mesh_topology&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:long_name = &quot;Topology data of 1D network&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:topology_dimension = 1 ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:node_coordinates = &quot;Mesh1_node_x Mesh1_node_y&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:edge_node_connectivity = &quot;Mesh1_edge_nodes&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1:edge_coordinates = &quot;Mesh1_edge_x Mesh1_edge_y&quot; ; // optional attribute<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span>integer Mesh1_edge_nodes(nMesh1_edge, Two) ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1_edge_nodes:cf_role = &quot;edge_node_connectivity&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1_edge_nodes:long_name = &quot;Maps every edge/link to the two nodes that it connects.&quot; ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>                </span>Mesh1_edge_nodes:start_index = 0 ; // default setting, attribute could have been skipped.<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>// Coordinate variables skipped<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>        </span><o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'>data:<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span
style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span><o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre><span

style='font-size:9.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>         </span>3,<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>4 ;<o:p></o:p></span></pre></div>

</div>

<div><pre><span style='font-size:9.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre><pre><span
